FROM [Fixture] AS [f]
INNER JOIN [League] AS [l] ON [f].[LeagueId] = [l].[LeagueId]
INNER JOIN [Club] AS [c] ON [f].[HomeTeamId] = [c].[ClubId]
INNER JOIN [Club] AS [c0] ON [f].[AwayTeamId] = [c0].[ClubId]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName], [a].[UserType], [a].[CreatedBy], [a].[CreatedDateTime], [a].[DateOfBirth], [a].[FirstName], [a].[IsActive], [a].[IsDeleted], [a].[IsFirstTimeLogin], [a].[IsSuspended], [a].[LastName], [a].[ModifiedBy], [a].[ModifiedDateTime], [a].[ProfilePicture], [a].[ClubId], [a].[ClubManager_ClubId], [a].[IsContractEnded], [a].[Player_ClubId], [a].[EndDate], [a].[IsContractSigned], [a].[JerseyNumber], [a].[MarketValue], [a].[PlayerCard], [a].[Position], [a].[StartDate]
    FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [a]
    WHERE [a].[UserType] IN (N'UserBaseModel', N'ClubAdministrator', N'ClubManager', N'Fan', N'Officials', N'Player', N'SportsMember', N'SystemAdministrator')
) AS [t] ON [f].[CreatedById] = [t].[Id]
